<h1 _ngcontent-dlq-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="双折叠"> 双折叠 </h1>

<div _ngcontent-dlq-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div id="body0000002352875141">    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 620px;">     <h2 id="section830871815913">概述<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section830871815913" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table212mcpsimp" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row216mcpsimp">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p219mcpsimp">折叠屏设备的三种形态分别为<strong>折叠态、展开态和悬停态</strong>。</p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p221mcpsimp">折叠态便于随身携带和单手操作，适合移动场景下的便捷使用；展开态屏幕变宽，能够充分展示应用内容，适合多任务处理和沉浸式体验；悬停态则处于完全展开和折叠的中间状态，设备可稳定放置，让用户解放双手。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p3927145813426"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163706.54572201873476280781068139868112:50001231000000:2800:A69915E768105AB004F20E2A6F02CFDB5751C60576A4AAF9EC7D1417FBC5A9FF.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 116px;">     <h2 id="section171032485916">基础要求<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section171032485916" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p225mcpsimp">为了保证以上体验，需要满足以下基础体验要求：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 962px;">     <h3 id="section1192143205911" class="firsth2">信息完整<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1192143205911" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul496mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li497mcpsimp">图片、视频等视觉元素不应发生变形、裁剪、显示不全等信息缺失。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li498mcpsimp">一般情况下，展开态不应出现页面内的内容元素数量减少，或图形化元素模糊、分辨率下降或视觉体量减小等损失，确保展开态的内容元素不少于折叠态内容元素信息量的3/4。</li>     </ul>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table499mcpsimp" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row504mcpsimp">         <td class="nocellnorowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1493917187447"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.46546813818163655087136629399673:50001231000000:2800:B83A6BD14BB210FB13A77FCAFE8388198D8FF9D6C358F5EBCAD27AB3FBEECFEB.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1544852212339"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.84545237085439172475132378271940:50001231000000:2800:6381D9310BFE63886D82E038228797BC359B320A82E63FF2284E64607C09A912.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p508mcpsimp">推荐</p></td>         <td class="cell-norowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p572402219455"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.20135992288344562475928557938014:50001231000000:2800:5585A13EB1552B83D1E9CBCBDDB7632C1C560AB3FB4321AFBFCFEB2E74F912C1.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1173031012483"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.19243485236026661989372778282466:50001231000000:2800:3AF04D26F8FD1C5A49C6FD553ECCF5BA920F688E215AAE7E2AEF6A0A8A2B3351.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p510mcpsimp">不推荐（图片过大导致一屏信息显示过少）</p></td>        </tr>        <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row511mcpsimp">         <td class="row-nocellborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p7760947104518"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.13692784211938920495655287989859:50001231000000:2800:E8A618A980685371F2C518ABE6029C232F03CC457752897B91620EF6E692C320.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p20423123611489"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.28846787199796187156503539788523:50001231000000:2800:AA4B84CF7D38BF7A391526A038EF1173D9BFB0312709602572221C6FA1F24AEF.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p515mcpsimp">推荐</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p28851134619"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163707.20335480708687299858022350879346:50001231000000:2800:4C2F51D941CEDDF0C13767F0A64CFB1C35B2CF40FC8EC8FA50748216E79CE432.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p142615218346"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163708.04798769249471571565163429048145:50001231000000:2800:0698F39A32565D0EF65FD6B8871246748265D42727075059C302B7CD38F26793.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p517mcpsimp">不推荐（内容放大导致一屏信息显示过少）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 576px;">     <h3 id="section2111137105912">交互跟手<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section2111137105912" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p494mcpsimp">折叠屏展开态屏幕尺寸较大，弹出框上的操作按钮不易触达。建议针对折叠屏展开态、平板等大尺寸的设备，提供跟手的弹出框。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1186410321469"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163708.85574344005197032449972445872067:50001231000000:2800:5EFE553308178BC4FB338659713FCDEAB2E984005117C276504B20C8FB0B19D4.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 688px;">     <h3 id="section971794214595">横屏适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section971794214595" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p521mcpsimp">折叠屏在展开态下的屏幕显示比例接近正方形，基于此特征，应用设计和开发时需要做如下考虑：</p>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul522mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li523mcpsimp">支持展开态横屏显示。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li524mcpsimp">展开态横竖屏布局一致。除部分特殊界面外，建议应用在横屏和竖屏下保持一样的布局。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li525mcpsimp">横竖屏旋转时，需要适配摄像头的挖孔区域，重要信息需要避开挖孔区显示。</li>     </ul>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p178584582465"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163708.11034171862196533363031368382976:50001231000000:2800:F2765B8B573859185C9264993F48733A933A65C28F606128F2F55638C5BC345F.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 648px;">     <h3 id="section168036495591">挖孔适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section168036495591" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p255mcpsimp">在设计界面布局时，应确保其适应摄像头挖孔区域，以确保重要信息不会在挖孔区域内显示。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p256mcpsimp">当设备处于竖向显示时，状态栏应避让挖孔区域；而在设备横向显示时，建议整列避让挖孔，对于一些固定且不会对内容产生影响的元素，如底部的标签栏，可以不进行避让。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p122539267474"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163708.93801774026520928188696438605936:50001231000000:2800:806749C2974048E1C682AEDAE8C3958FB182AFD170FBC5B518A0F94CD523D2D3.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 523px;">     <h3 id="section197165912599">文字适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section197165912599" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p432mcpsimp">在折叠屏设备的展开态，图标和字体大小应保持与折叠态一致，以确保良好的可读性和用户体验。若确需调整，建议控制在1.2倍以内。单屏文本长度建议控制在36字左右，最长不超过40字。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table433mcpsimp" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row438mcpsimp">         <td class="row-nocellborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14816195274714"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163708.65190185857739574351821108067099:50001231000000:2800:28B34974215B6E64EDFF5DCB4DE5CB25FCC3B52A0ED6BC080609EB0F8730F2AE.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1618501712351"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.00574252075932607714427599202641:50001231000000:2800:3098BE640338FA82FA5CD29D31931EE199A62C6BC72855CA8443B33C56B08207.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p4181314448">推荐</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p82754484913"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.40582822553608800913493528785377:50001231000000:2800:18B6838842BF0D061680DAD439BE44F2009ECF0AF7A594A0692D00CB41AAC537.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p11646112153613"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.91667498191780160419374115456539:50001231000000:2800:2F9401C12C0E2D25931A0824D597A883A2C1C2337E625645DB19C5A488E1110D.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="1.8261780104712042"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14337122012415">不推荐（字体过大导致一屏幕显示的信息太少）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3094px;">     <h3 id="section139254419012">图标适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section139254419012" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p132mcpsimp">展开态图标大小不应发生明显变化，建议保持跟折叠态一样的大小。若一定要发生大小变化，则最大不要超过1.2倍。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p133mcpsimp">折叠屏展开态入口图标显示主要有相对拉伸、挪移布局、延伸布局、相对拉伸&amp;挪移布局四种方式。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p134mcpsimp">(1) 相对拉伸：折叠屏展开后，入口图标数量不变、大小不变、布局不变，图标间距均匀变宽。但需要避免图标左右边距过大或图标之间间距过大。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table234465310355" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row33441353133517">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p173441538357"><span><img originheight="1240" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.71819278660762066046025928756871:50001231000000:2800:4B06C4D2BEE7C2036623EFE4D552E0BFA1FF60B51C7AC2EB0D3DC422B33E7928.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="300.931744312026"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p452531462010"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.31294650395097671088363346578937:50001231000000:2800:F6EB30CE46B0A91878EB13B82A9C33DFF8FE806E51F36F6A50BB4217C23C714C.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p912917491416">推荐（图标相对拉伸）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p141mcpsimp">(2) 挪移布局：折叠屏展开后，图标使用挪移布局，入口图标3行变2行，横向平铺。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table0502161893716" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row1950291813377">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p7502518103715"><span><img originheight="1240" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.38234438338844927709689443243388:50001231000000:2800:22CDDBD30E3AC8241067FA5AF02DB07EE15845A56EB96721703A7F6591175BC1.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="300.931744312026"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p650219185370"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.51674773327693536104131346211592:50001231000000:2800:0597EE839560F1780DBEEB80E5A3191A38E28CD99E4B1FFA54DB8C2494B2C198.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p2936102511519">推荐（图标挪移布局且适当调整间距）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p143mcpsimp">(3) 延伸布局：折叠屏展开后，图标使用延伸布局，一屏内显示更多图标数量，用户可以横滑显示更多。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table599336153812" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row109931266380">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p59939663818"><span><img originheight="1240" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.26172623602779362807081791326209:50001231000000:2800:E67305DD34409A7D6EA2A89F62820C996853C14ACE78C8C0389C2ECE88EA83B5.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="300.931744312026"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p7993126153819"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163709.21024820013777184502155350125783:50001231000000:2800:A004FEFECF18FBAB0E616C65FBAF6EC2C06D9E616A613536673443E06E0BA2C5.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p887314519516">推荐（图标延伸布局且适当调整间距）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p145mcpsimp">(4) 相对拉伸&amp;挪移布局：折叠态图标数量固定时，折叠屏展开后图标间距相对拉伸，大小不变，建议文字部分进行挪移布局，图标在左，文字在右，以避免图标信息过疏。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table101071579394" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p147mcpsimp">(5) 以下3种为图标适配中常见的显示效果不佳的案例。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 80px;">     <h2 id="section49814121304">组件适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section49814121304" </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1784px;">     <h3 id="section321923917011">组合控件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section321923917011" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p269mcpsimp"><strong>顶部搜索框+子页签/其他控件</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p271mcpsimp">(1) 相对拉伸：折叠屏展开后，按钮、图标等元素大小不变，间距横向均匀变宽。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table1554132124517" style="border-style: none;" </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p273mcpsimp">(2) 延伸布局：折叠屏展开后，控件元素的大小不变，间距均匀变宽，可显示的页签数量增多。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p275mcpsimp">(3) 挪移布局：折叠屏展开后，由于横向空间明显增加，组合控件内的元素由原来上下排布的两行变为左右排布的一行。变为一行后，可根据优先级对内容进行先后排序。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p445220441117">推荐（一级和二级工具栏同时延伸布局且相对拉伸）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table1673810254487" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row8738725134814">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 7461px;">     <h3 id="section11201057309">运营类图片/视频/卡片<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section11201057309" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p448mcpsimp">运营类的图片/视频等，通常有卡片和沉浸式两种样式。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p449mcpsimp">展开态的图片/视频/卡片应适应页面的宽度、间距、列数等因素进行适配显示，不能造成信息量的明显减少或信息密度过大。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p450mcpsimp"><strong>居中的运营类图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul452mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li453mcpsimp">折叠态显示单张居中的卡片，折叠屏展开后，可横向延伸显示两张或三张运营卡片。</li>     </ul>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table21811732135012" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table4405174455214" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row114051144105219">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p459mcpsimp"><strong>首页的沉浸式运营类图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p461mcpsimp">应用首页的沉浸式的图片/视频/卡片在展开态显示过大，是折叠屏适配中较为常见的问题。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p462mcpsimp">（1）针对有多张沉浸广告图的，展开后，横向平铺显示多张广告图。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table13971323175313" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row097102314538">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14979232534"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163713.79557273516691563324577233562340:50001231000000:2800:BF8ED537006D97E0EA1DD9AB10DB03847C74F4A19764482F5409E2C1BCFF3CD6.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="495.08125677139765"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p398162365313"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163714.50265401506747593290194287084073:50001231000000:2800:EE123CA2DBAE3C3F67EB35D8A0A57151A3D444EA54D11A3749458AEAF54C0DCE.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p5625132991715">推荐（一排平铺显示多张沉浸式广告图）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p464mcpsimp">（2）针对只有单张沉浸广告图的，宽高比大于2∶1的沉浸式广告，折叠屏展开后，整体内容等比放大。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table12297153195315" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row16297115315531">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1929725312537"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163714.39756765471390443024948317094517:50001231000000:2800:AE5B7BEF24BC04E56D269A43DA1E831E9697C57EB424E7492FE2BD1A43E1CA4A.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="495.08125677139765"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1629795345310"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163714.84681259784514168107683449718496:50001231000000:2800:F3465D21C74B6FD4A93F0FD02D19CC3F9286E86D0BA2D03CD599F96FADF788E6.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p13309947151712">推荐（宽高比大于2∶1且只有单张沉浸式广告图，展开态等比放大广告图，确保不超过屏幕的1/2高度）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p466mcpsimp">（3）针对只有单张沉浸广告图的，宽高比小于2∶1的沉浸式广告，建议将背景图和广告内容元素分层。折叠屏展开后，背景图等比放大的同时顶部和底部适当裁剪。避免裁剪到核心信息，同时确保广告背景图的高度不超过屏幕高度的1/2，广告内容的核心元素可适当放大。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table1656915319220" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p6722328181810">推荐（宽高比小于2∶1且只有单张沉浸式广告图，背景图进行智能裁剪，核心元素适当放大，确保不超过屏幕的1/2高度）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table2036181217318" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row2361151217313">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p43618124316"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692"  </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p469mcpsimp">（4）针对有按钮、页签等控件的沉浸广告图，建议将背景图和广告内容元素分层。展开后，背景图横向撑满且高度不变，按原来布局基于响应式规则调整内容元素的大小。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table122181116419" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row62181411144">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p6218619413"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163714.68950741762167942114512987009916:50001231000000:2800:51B9AFBF4C6F2DE2EAA0EA7AA94045DCCCF68433F8246F0CB2AAED945088DDDE.png" </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p471mcpsimp"><strong>详情页的沉浸式运营类图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p473mcpsimp">部分应用详情页使用较大的沉浸式图片/视频/卡片展示商品详情，用于吸引用户。在该页面，需要确保展开态时，广告内容能显示完全，且商品的核心信息不被裁剪。通常建议在展开态通过显示多张广告图来解决宽屏适配问题。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table1271172012511" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row5271320758">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1627122012513"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692" idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row185616281065">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p108561284610"><span><img originheight="2040" originwidth="3692" </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 11446px;">     <h3 id="section91191920210">内容类图片/视频/卡片<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section91191920210" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p303mcpsimp">折叠屏展开态内容的显示主要有瀑布流或宫格布局、信息流布局两种形式。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p304mcpsimp"><strong>瀑布流或宫格布局的图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul306mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li307mcpsimp">横向的图片/视频/卡片，在展开态建议增加1列。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li308mcpsimp">竖向的图片/视频/卡片，在展开态建议增加1列或2列。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li309mcpsimp">瀑布流或宫格布局的图片/视频/卡片，在展开态的列数至少不低于2列，至多不超过6列。</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li310mcpsimp">若该瀑布流或宫格布局的内容，在展开态不增加列数，则需要确保单个图片/视频/卡片的高度不超过1/2屏幕高度。</li>     </ul>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table6126151815106" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row121261118201015">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14126918171011"><span><img originheight="1512" originwidth="3692"     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p318mcpsimp"><strong>社交类信息流布局的图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p320mcpsimp">此类信息流布局，从折叠到展开需要重点考虑图片/视频/卡片的适配，并区分首页和详情页两种情况。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p321mcpsimp">首页或该页面有多条信息流的：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p322mcpsimp">（1）9宫格聚合图片/视频/卡片，建议不低于1/2屏幕高度，不超过60%屏幕高度，约为55%屏幕高度最佳；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p323mcpsimp">（2）单张横向或方形图片/视频/卡片，建议不低于1/3屏幕高度，不超过40%屏幕高度；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p324mcpsimp">（3）单张竖向图片/视频/卡片，建议不低于1/3屏幕高度，不超过60%屏幕高度，约为50%屏幕高度最佳；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p325mcpsimp">详情页或该页面仅极少条信息流内容的，信息流中的单张图片/视频/卡片或多张聚合的图片，高度建议不超过屏幕高度的60%。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table87072532152" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row1370716533151">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p67071853121519"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" title="点击放大" width="896" height="517.8938244853738"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p18973104194118"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163719.84532039765962699932244059147326:50001231000000:2800:E618C440A4485692AD3F47400A0031F86FAB7286FB59182852D4075BA3AF3BE8.png"      </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table17455521615" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1061192571614"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row6854165818189">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1485420583185"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163720.62545151951623442334778780546221:50001231000000:2800:D7D3EE533026FA146520ED1467B8A91DBF6814B76D7348C68C8C2D47FCF6E18C.png" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163720.87495860227825112037083066593530:50001231000000:2800:BED2C03221A8B2EBCDAA32D5193F4605E9B30E1BC53809448F631F0966763EE8.png" </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p330mcpsimp"><strong>新闻资讯类信息流布局的图片/视频/卡片</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p332mcpsimp">此类信息流布局，从折叠到展开需要重点考虑图片/视频/卡片的适配，并区分首页和详情页两种情况。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p333mcpsimp">首页或该页面有多条信息流的：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p334mcpsimp">（1）单张方形或竖向图片/视频/卡片，建议不超过60%屏幕高度；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p335mcpsimp">（2）单张横向图片/视频/卡片，建议不超过40%屏幕高度；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p336mcpsimp">（3）有多张图片/视频/卡片时，建议平铺显示。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p337mcpsimp">详情页信息流中的图片/视频/卡片，建议不超过60%屏幕高度，有多张连续的图片/视频/卡片时，建议其横向平铺。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p338mcpsimp">点击图片/视频/卡片后，全屏显示图片/视频时，需要确保默认一屏幕内显示完整的图片/视频内容。特殊的超长广告图除外。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table15238112531915" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row1123852511195">         <td </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1288px;">     <h3 id="section186714110114">弹出框<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section186714110114" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p208mcpsimp">弹出框在应用设计中较为常见，例如红包、广告等，建议展开态和折叠态弹出框保持相同的大小，或大小变化最大不超过1.2倍。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table1251465882212" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row105141258162215">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1051416586229"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163722.24635926030940816047055379857624:50001231000000:2800:CF80D46DD0B269A1FBA30B3BE503B9C2DCF992990F36F43E92EDBFF935E10AD9.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="517.8938244853738"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1951405802213"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163723.01567987346198878443040195049483:50001231000000:2800:A3C5BA50D28339547488F309118BC92C22B01B7B2C2ED90C9A883AD69B851BD7.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p9115930202612">推荐（弹窗大小不变）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table5220163022318" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row1622013017236">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p15220183015237"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163723.42380830397081708211055025783296:50001231000000:2800:C3E5FB87E5451DBD90C1618EE1FFA5A35A657A19B766907BD9B2D9EE11765240.png" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163723.53233801047982283565003996108263:50001231000000:2800:1DC8A6C1925F3967A5743281D5C6011A6A250B05BD420FC363F95327DE0328B2.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1598145019268">不推荐（展开态弹出框过大，导致显示不全或无法交互）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 696px;">     <h3 id="section5715147118">其他控件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5715147118" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p446mcpsimp">页面中的其他界面元素，例如按钮、输入框等，建议展开折叠时高度按照字体大小的缩放比例进行缩放，或大小变化最大不超过1.2倍，宽度根据元素本身的响应式规则进行设计，部分元素（例如按钮）保持等比缩放，部分元素（例如列表、输入框）对宽度进行适当延伸，最宽不超过整个窗口的宽度。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p49210227129"><span><img originheight="2134" originwidth="3692" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163723.22683890871340845382777366422114:50001231000000:2800:DF536F07BDC266589D48907ED4CF23C6B44C52E1379581EE92E0495EEB09D66D.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="531.7659804983748"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 116px;">     <h2 id="section5560057912">开合接续<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5560057912" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14111663711">在折叠态和展开态切换时，应确保页面不发生跳转，焦点不发生偏移。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1908px;">     <h3 id="section5635102111217" class="firsth2">页面不跳转<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5635102111217" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p372mcpsimp">展开态不应出现页面跳转、操作步骤增加，操作更复杂等体验下降的情况。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p373mcpsimp">不应破坏应用内原有的沉浸式体验，避免仅仅为了扩充内容，或强制应用分屏而过度改变用户体验和用户习惯。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p374mcpsimp">在折叠态和展开态之间切换时，需要保证当前任务的连续性。切换前的任务和相关状态应能够保存、延续或快速恢复，以提供连续的用户体验，避免出现闪退、重启等异常情况。</p>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul375mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li376mcpsimp">页面内容，均需要支持开合接续；</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li377mcpsimp">弹出层控件，且点击周边空白区域自动关闭的，可以开合不接续，例如弹出框、toast 等；</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li378mcpsimp">半模态控件需要支持开合接续。</li>     </ul>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table19734191382410" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row67341113182411">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p16734151319247"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163723.44051743327785399314817177183780:50001231000000:2800:1F9041CFF015142DDE8A13A60C11C833BC5036BF6B98D79370AE3D4F1B8226E3.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="448"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p153221933184412"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.59187926127222169253436034407501:50001231000000:2800:4137C9F60AB07306036A388673A2EFB0475C11487D72C888C92E699DCBE038DB.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p2761913142717">推荐 (拍摄状态和参数不变)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table3599103312249" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row115991833202413">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1559918334245"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.80693444245227976405455197843368:50001231000000:2800:B6A862C396289CAD77D63128B5492F19192AC536651715040DA1F6E3633BC017.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="448"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p16599233182418"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.76374605265337466152223127448471:50001231000000:2800:4334DCEBAB74B906046A378CDB08A316BEAE4524A1777936C40E4B4C3D1329A0.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p5496729132717">推荐 (阅读的焦点不偏移)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table35658532511" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row115659582517">         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="100%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p65651253252"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.21823882826860707479220821683647:50001231000000:2800:8626E49C982972B96B9314609596B020BE1A078FB12EBA3C58E751EC8F823A0F.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="448"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p4259498456"><span><img originheight="8" originwidth="1910" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.90795199213035487275854696911778:50001231000000:2800:47FA67485556DF268583BB85D08A6D6C40D0C82182A30CBBA70A8951A44BE046.png" title="点击放大" width="896" height="3.7528795811518325"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p866017444276">不推荐 (页面跳转，任务中断)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2172px;">     <h3 id="section19331162817210">焦点不偏移<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section19331162817210" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p292mcpsimp">当有足够多的显示内容时，第一个完整的信息作为接续的起始位置，例如下图的卡片 7 作为接续的起始位置。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p8162734143"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163724.64528298025484992154250687038666:50001231000000:2800:B74350F964BF8CB1737441349C50BA774D89814D033251737F57F9ADA8310C9E.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p293mcpsimp">当显示的内容不足一排时，以当前态看到的第一个内容，作为另一个状态的起始行内容。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p83531019101418"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163725.47562678799112482265886384300972:50001231000000:2800:9DDC1B93481B9D5B70F83BF805FF1192BC1EC7D7410C87181D143A0A37C88FF1.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p294mcpsimp">支持左右横滑的内容，开合接续时，左侧第一个完整的内容作为另一个状态的起始位置。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p197243201412"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163725.77193133627866602297507025195469:50001231000000:2800:F39E12698791A6F18C91545EF698F2A64CD97F13B8E7C3ED739891872D33B591.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p295mcpsimp">当支持左右横滑的内容，在另外一个状态遇到末尾数据时，右侧内容填满。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1763184441416"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163725.77045611955694213062193947949129:50001231000000:2800:82D617441B7E73EE5209606FD2067BA4BF628C67875D290E5FDB45AB3550D60E.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 164px;">     <h2 id="section117720445215">交互架构<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section117720445215" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p942019267380">在大屏幕设备上，双页面同时显示为用户提供了创新的操作体验。当应用程序中的两个页面存在关联关系时，可以考虑采用组合页面的方式。根据不同的场景需求，选择合适的页面组合关系至关重要。组合页面主要包括以下三种类型：层级关系、主从关系和并列关系。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2113px;">     <h3 id="section1619215511122" class="firsth2">层级关系<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1619215511122" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p227mcpsimp">层级关系可以分为多层级和单一层级两种类型。层级关系的双窗口展示方式通常被称为分栏。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p354148163919"><strong>多层级分栏</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p183mcpsimp">在多层级分栏结构中，存在一个完整的多层结构，例如复杂的系统设置菜单、海量内容（如综合电商的商品、视频、图片或音乐的媒体资源、新闻网站的海量新闻）的门户及多级分类子页面。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p184mcpsimp">这种交互方式的特点如下：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p185mcpsimp">第一级的基础分类通常以列表形式呈现，以便用户能够快速了解整个结构的概览。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p186mcpsimp">末级列表页面中的元素为最小内容元素，例如单个商品、单个媒体素材、单条新闻等。这使得用户能够更方便地访问和操作具体的信息。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1230420314164"><span><img originheight="1821" originwidth="4096" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163725.44295030034686512834720968384409:50001231000000:2800:7C50F2C4C84D8287B0A1BEE90EE69CA1ADD2291A4B1C85FA183E1EC8F0A419D8.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="409.013671875"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p319965121610">      </p><div class="video-box" style="width: 920px; height: 458.16px;"><div                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p190mcpsimp">有多个层级递进关系的场景示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p4541194419393"><strong>单一层级分栏</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p152mcpsimp">单一层级结构通常采用“列表+详情”的形式展示，其中列表中的每个元素均为末端元素，不包含二级分类列表。这种结构适用于邮件、信息、备忘录等类型的内容元素列表。此类交互的特点如下：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p153mcpsimp">列表中仅包含独立的元素，无子列表，左右两侧内容属性固定，有助于减少用户迷失。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p154mcpsimp">用户点击左侧列表中的某个条目时，右侧将显示对应的详情内容。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p155mcpsimp">用户可通过在左侧列表中点击任意一个条目，快速在右侧打开对应的详情内容，实现内容的快速切换。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p16921153411814">      </p><div class="video-box"                         </svg></i>
                      </div></div></div></div><p></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2234px;">     <h3 id="section1650917571329">主从关系<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1650917571329" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p346mcpsimp">在主从关系类型中，一侧的主导页面为沉浸式场景，而另一侧的辅助页面则呈现评论、互动讨论、参考信息等相关内容。根据沉浸内容的情况，主从关系可以分为左右或上下的组合页面结构。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p347mcpsimp">主从关系的交互逻辑特点如下：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p348mcpsimp">两部分之间相互独立，且具有明显的主从关系。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p349mcpsimp">辅助侧依赖主导侧存在，若主导侧关闭或切换，辅助侧页面不能单独存在，需同步关闭或切换。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p350mcpsimp">主导侧的内容呈现不受打扰和中断，持续保持最佳的沉浸状态。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p351mcpsimp">辅助侧的内容用户可以进行滚动浏览，适合于信息流数据，用户可参与互动。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p352mcpsimp">主从关系的信息架构样式主要有以下几种，应用可根据具体场景进行选择：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p41811040194012"><strong>悬浮面板</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p478mcpsimp">从属信息默认以悬浮面板的形式显示，通过特定按钮或特定手势交互触发，一般用于作为主要信息的筛选项或更多菜单项，不影响主要信息的展示。</p>                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p192mcpsimp">短视频应用使用侧边栏的示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 670px;">     <h3 id="section15423241737">并列关系<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section15423241737" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p383mcpsimp">在并列关系中，界面中的两侧内容具有同等的重要性。这些内容可以是同类型的内容，也可以是不同类型的内容。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p384mcpsimp">例如，在购物应用中，下单前对两个相似商品进行详细对比的页面属于同类型内容的并列；而购物应用中一侧窗口显示商品信息，另一侧显示与商家的对话界面，则属于不同类型内容的并列。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p385mcpsimp">并列关系有助于用户更详细地比较两个商品的信息，或进行更高效的交互操作。在这种组合页面中，左右两页面之间不存在主次和从属关系，页面分割比例应为1:1。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table386mcpsimp" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row391mcpsimp">         <td class="nocellnorowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="49%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1935453912218"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163726.34885716547627298387071032352280:50001231000000:2800:1ECE6E97D994EB2AEF85E66D6291D01AF29C3958F6CB587000E129E642233C01.png" title="点击放大" width="426.8" height="320.1"></span></p></td>         <td class="cell-norowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="51%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p65801158132120"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163726.62549897028544865472969742286861:50001231000000:2800:CFC57006FBD2693C3576EEAD68B32AB4DA5A056A6DC17C42D4B9BAF731A2EFC4.png" title="点击放大" width="445.2" height="333.9"></span></p></td>        </tr>        <tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row393mcpsimp">         <td class="row-nocellborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="49%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p395mcpsimp"><strong>相同类型内容的页面并列</strong></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p397mcpsimp">两边有相同的页面布局、各段信息相互对应</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="51%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p399mcpsimp"><strong>不同类型内容的页面并列</strong></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p401mcpsimp">两边页面布局和内容不同，但相互间有关联性</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 140px;">     <h2 id="section2352012733">响应式布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section2352012733" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p356mcpsimp">随着屏幕设备规格的变化，界面中所呈现的信息量有增加，常见的响应式布局的表现形式为：相对拉伸、相对缩放、延伸布局、挪移布局、重复布局、瀑布布局等。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 600px;">     <h3 id="section1777012183313" class="firsth2">相对拉伸<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1777012183313" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p176mcpsimp">布局特点：页面内元素的显示宽度不是固定值，而是通过相对参照物的方式来确定其开始和结束的位置。当布局的显示大小发生变化时，元素的显示宽度随之发生改变。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p44332313221"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163726.86814094477442340841720815146942:50001231000000:2800:BE9E2199D0B4B0FE0B95295C6198883C4CC76F42EC486A3A7D5BCDFE1EBD06F9.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 600px;">     <h3 id="section4944271134">相对缩放<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4944271134" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p198mcpsimp">布局特点：布局内元素的显示大小不是固定值，而是通过相对参照物的方式来确定其宽或者高的参数。当布局的显示大小发生变化时，元素的大小随之发生缩放。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p14229163814223"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163726.84317398953584389629979052074073:50001231000000:2800:5CA5C4E5F75A7ABBFC488497C51271369D6EC78303D53B4A88131F01720FA05F.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 672px;">     <h3 id="section6223341534">延伸布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section6223341534" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p102mcpsimp">布局特点：组件内元素横向布局，元素间的距离固定，可显示元素的数量可随着显示宽度的改变而变化。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p121139106232">适用场景：内容呈现型界面，单页面内信息架构扁平，内容元素为单层列表或分组列表结构，例如内容门户网站首页面。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1311381042318">适配规则：保持页面元素尺寸或间距不变，随着屏幕宽度的增加，在横向显示更多元素。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p6157058122312"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163727.81375864106694497059558599800267:50001231000000:2800:491B246AACA7F3A1A9CBA31EE96E173D5B3C2FF36A16512E6E5F71B862E7665C.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 696px;">     <h3 id="section75391113912">挪移布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section75391113912" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p251mcpsimp">布局特点：布局内的元素根据布局的宽度来选择是上下排布还是左右排布。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p18499283233">适用场景：页面内信息架构层级少的，例如门户网站首页面、内容详情页面等。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p6849142872315">适配规则：首先判断布局区域是否有明显的“宽高特征”，即横纵比是否大于4:3；其次判断横向宽度，是否能容得下若干个元素，如果容得下就左右排布，容不下就上下排布。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p9264101514247"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163727.82286691200789971954515933902617:50001231000000:2800:7366029B61232FB95679C19ED92C30371B8757DB7436616CE2C6BCC0F80CA3CE.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 696px;">     <h3 id="section58942066910">重复布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section58942066910" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p178mcpsimp">布局特点：利用屏幕的宽度优势，将相同属性的布局组件横向并列同时排布。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p2272136182317">适用场景：内容运营类列表信息，例如歌单列表、应用列表等。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p42721636202319">适配规则：可以定义单个元素的宽度规则，随着屏幕宽度的变化，⾃动计算可以重复的元素的个数，满足宽度条件时横向重复排列。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p87149972519"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163727.37046773350892814053654434985096:50001231000000:2800:C9F314C9301BFF22C57A4D900E16EC82B7ACA5134D4BFCC7E1DF0A64743E5B85.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 672px;">     <h3 id="section841721313916">瀑布布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section841721313916" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p538mcpsimp">布局特点：利用屏幕的宽度优势，将原来单列纵向布局，拓展为两列或多列的纵向布局。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p3248144112239">适用场景：适合用卡片呈现内容的场景，通过卡片的横纵扩展在⼤屏上展示更多内容。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1824854118238">适配规则：可以定义单个组件的宽度规则，随着页面宽度的变化，⾃动计算可以重复的卡片个数，满足条件时横向排列更多卡片。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p0177152942516"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163727.10221490335576602995185650255407:50001231000000:2800:FE66962F5AF6295DA0A6AE2DEE1BC456179A6B7D734FC87758F2E5CA1CB9A37E.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 316px;">     <h2 id="section9507193611476">布局&amp;交互创新<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section9507193611476" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p364mcpsimp">结合六种动态布局规则，三种双页面交互架构规则以及多窗交互规则，在折叠屏上可以进行多种布局样式和交互的创新设计，以下为一些参考范式。</p>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__ul365mcpsimp">      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li366mcpsimp">分栏布局</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li367mcpsimp">挪移布局</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li368mcpsimp">重复布局</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li369mcpsimp">瀑布流&amp;宫格布局</li>      <li id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__li370mcpsimp">临时双窗</li>     </ul>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 648px;">     <h3 id="section828065434712" class="firsth2">分栏布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section828065434712" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p281mcpsimp">分栏布局是一种具有层级关系的左右分窗口设计，其主要目的是在宽屏设备上实现良好的视觉效果，从而提高用户的任务处理效率。这种布局方式特别适用于文件管理、联系人、设置、备忘录等应用程序的展开状态。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1172315102612"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163728.36871135856356688558897773412900:50001231000000:2800:ECD2930177645CDCA018EC407B2110F4859D41EC4B669281AD3A63568F500C3F.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p282mcpsimp">备忘录的分栏布局示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3692px;">     <h3 id="section115016034812">挪移布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section115016034812" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p110mcpsimp">通过调整折叠屏设备的布局，从折叠状态到展开状态，可以实现布局的挪移变化，从而提高阅读舒适度和浏览效率。以下是四种常见的挪移布局用法。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p111mcpsimp"><strong>范式1：将不同页面的内容整合到同一页的布局调整。</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p113mcpsimp"><strong>边看边评</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p115mcpsimp">在阅读时，展开状态下同时显示文章详情和评论列表，满足用户在阅读文章的同时查看评论的需求。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1958323152617"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163728.33818097825956786735390495831748:50001231000000:2800:C727CFE13F1AF6E465372F3A742003942F45126A634760A22C2B5D329D0E5498.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p116mcpsimp">边看新闻边看评论的示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p117mcpsimp"><strong>范式2：同一页面的上下结构内容，变成左右结构的挪移布局。</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p119mcpsimp"><strong>杂志排版</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p121mcpsimp">本范式常用于阅读场景的图片和文本之间的挪移布局。不仅能解决图片过大的问题，还能通过杂志化布局带来更好的视觉效果。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p227020319287"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163728.09640829229675528027651039374972:50001231000000:2800:10159BE6FCEDD03F315090A7D3668E69D00364622BD892C192245D17BC73CA5A.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p122mcpsimp">同一页面的新闻，从上下图文变成左右图文的挪移布局示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1089192018286"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163728.48120649937404214181524534390787:50001231000000:2800:1F31805023D93B7949F701EF0AFAAE189866C958690E818DA24E4421DEB3F557.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p123mcpsimp">同一页面的生活服务信息，从上下图文变成左右图文的挪移布局示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p124mcpsimp"><strong>范式3：有层级结构的图文内容，变成左右结构的挪移布局。</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p8899175717284"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163729.87099931399352789186713337108625:50001231000000:2800:D845339C7F92D0ADD08013091B2B0E9C1D42ED7B95EA0DCCD866FEE1B262B9D8.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p126mcpsimp">首页的图文内容，从层叠变成左右图文的挪移布局示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p127mcpsimp"><strong>范式4：通过挪移布局，在展开态上减少次要信息对核心信息的干扰。</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1986542942913"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163729.37194327366828832535941140954428:50001231000000:2800:0F93389CDA6B9745005B0B1D9673947ABC44FCF6BD504416CE13BB9FA099E0DF.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p129mcpsimp">看视频时，弹幕和操作按钮挪移布局到周边空闲区域的示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p679214515299"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163729.80023601802258043174872288039504:50001231000000:2800:E3FE9D0DFF9556281C77A39EC4991DAD405D334FC2514EC279CB36DD15424790.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p130mcpsimp">多人视频通话时，参会人信息从底部挪移到展开态的侧边，减少对视频通话画面遮挡的示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1225px;">     <h3 id="section45704180488">重复布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section45704180488" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p200mcpsimp">折叠屏设备，从折叠到展开，页面内的列表、卡片等均可通过重复布局，横向展示更多信息，提升页面的浏览效率，同时避免信息过疏。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p3171703265"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4330" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163730.88142941885525075912319935363062:50001231000000:2800:688728428337179DB3FB7D468C780197B9EE591A4963E557C52F7F91DAE3ADEB.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="458.9376443418014"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p201mcpsimp">列表在展开态重复布局的示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p202mcpsimp">从折叠态到展开态，使用重复布局时，通常内容按照从左到右的Z字形排布。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1932092912614">      </p><div class="video-box" style="width: 920px;                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p206mcpsimp">卡片在展开态重复布局的视频示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1900px;">     <h3 id="section109695121011">瀑布流&amp;宫格布局<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section109695121011" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p160mcpsimp">瀑布流布局适用于卡片式结构。折叠态的单列卡片，到展开态显示双列卡片，不同高度的卡片形成错落有致的瀑布流布局。可以有效提升页面的浏览效率和可视化效果。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p161mcpsimp">新闻首页卡片瀑布流布局示例</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p162mcpsimp">瀑布流布局和卡片的重复布局比较相似，内容也按照从左到右的Z字形排布，卡片的高度可以不同。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p138076633116">      </p><div class="video-box"                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p174mcpsimp">双指缩放进行宫格布局调整的视频示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3079px;">     <h3 id="section1458141710109">临时双窗<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1458141710109" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p279mcpsimp">播放视频或购物类场景，通常使用临时双窗口来实现“边看边评”或“边看边买”的体验。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p169652216514"><strong>边看边评</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p235mcpsimp">播放视频时，点击评论按钮，在不影响视频播放等核心任务的前提下，为评论留出足够的空间，从而实现一边看视频一边看评论或边看边写评论的体验。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p4451945112720">      </p><div                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p536mcpsimp">看直播时通过临时双窗口完成购物及支付的示例</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p56619318539">折叠屏设备因其大屏特性，天然具备多窗口适配的优势。这种多窗口交互方式能够显著提高信息处理效率，特别适用于需要同时处理多个任务的场景。通过充分利用屏幕空间，用户可以实现多任务的高效协同，从而显著提升工作效率。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 646px;">     <h3 id="section11834340171015" class="firsth2">悬浮窗<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section11834340171015" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p258mcpsimp">可通过悬浮窗显示需要临时使用的任务，全屏显示需要长时间使用的任务，从而实现任务的短暂并行或快速处理。实现临时任务处理。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p468885219391">      </p><div                       </div></div></div></div><p></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p262mcpsimp">示例：调出支付悬浮窗快速完成支付，避免页面跳转</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 648px;">     <h3 id="section8456144951013">分屏<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section8456144951013" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p358mcpsimp">分屏功能适用于需要同时运行两个应用的多任务场景，支持左右分屏和上下分屏两种样式，在大尺寸设备上可提供无遮挡的高效任务并行体验。例如，用户可以边逛商品边比价、边看视频边聊天、边学视频边记笔记。</p>     <p class="msonormal" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p359mcpsimp"><span><img originheight="3240" originwidth="6480" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163730.29938562515444780958579540272752:50001231000000:2800:9C8B86B1099B131C8DC364708A23FD2AA7F18C79B3CC4A392468D1B3DAB3DFC3.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p360mcpsimp">示例：边看视频边聊天</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 622px;">     <h3 id="section04591553100">跨屏拖拽<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section04591553100" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p264mcpsimp">在形成分屏或打开悬浮窗后，用户可以从一个窗口内拖拽内容到另一个窗口。这个功能支持内容的跨应用传递，例如将文字、图片、视频或链接从一个窗口拖拽到另一个窗口，从而实现高效的内容交互，进一步提升多任务处理的效率和灵活性。</p>     <p                         </svg></i>
                      </div></div></div></div><p></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 140px;">     <h2 id="section183378919119">悬停态<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section183378919119" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p403mcpsimp">折叠屏产品支持独特的悬停态，即产品半折后立于桌面，实现免手持的便捷体验。悬停态适用于无需频繁交互的场景，如观看视频、视频通话、拍照及听歌等。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 763px;">     <h3 id="section3969613141113" class="firsth2">悬停态适配<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section3969613141113" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p410mcpsimp">悬停态时，持握和放置状态下，手指最舒适的操作热区均集中在下半屏，而上半屏的可视角度更加友好。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p411mcpsimp">悬停状态下，屏幕按照交互的难易程度，可分为以下四个部分：</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p412mcpsimp">1 易操作区：在此区域内，手指交互操作稳定舒适，一般在此区域放置关键交互操作，例如按钮、拖动条等；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p413mcpsimp">2 不易操作区：在此区域内，手指交互时不太容易直接触达，需要更多地伸展手指或发生持握方式的变化</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p414mcpsimp">3 难操作区或显示区：在此区域内，执行触屏交互容易导致设备不稳定，一般不在此区域呈现交互类控件，或将此区域作为显示区，呈现浏览型内容，例如图片、视频等；</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p415mcpsimp">4 无法操作区：该区域一般为设备的悬停夹角区域。该区域操作精准度低，且显示内容容易变形，应尽量避免在此区域放置交互操作或显示重要信息；建议在上下半屏分别预留一定的空白区域。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__table416mcpsimp" style="border-style: none;" class="layoutFixed idpTab">               <tbody><tr id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__row421mcpsimp">         <td class="row-nocellborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p7761154917406"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163731.14607146261060290724348734909241:50001231000000:2800:3185055BB9983934D8DD0211536C44F37071ED8529F9BDD0B16C63FB9B42C40B.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p422mcpsimp">悬停态双手持握</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="border: none;" valign="top" width="50%">          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p167314224112"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="2880" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163731.96860471353505801493789286605733:50001231000000:2800:789288A9BC55053C1928267271A35EE10C1FD73F3332F6A108388A3769F0F26E.png" title="点击放大" width="436" height="327"></span></p>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p424mcpsimp">悬停态半折平放</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 600px;">     <h3 id="section15688112961114">悬停态折痕避让规格<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section15688112961114" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p297mcpsimp">悬停态时，中间弯折区域难以操作且显示内容会变形，因此建议页面内容进行折痕区避让适配。建议上半屏内容由中线向上避让16vp（3毫米）、下半屏内容由中线向下避让40vp（7毫米）。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p142041211114115"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163731.26071983891805280993098854282826:50001231000000:2800:E10E29316D9C3028CFE743CF1B1B4B8FF244FD2F6303D563EE765D238D175AA4.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 6080px;">     <h3 id="section12307164615117">典型悬停适配案例<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section12307164615117" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p223mcpsimp">悬停状态下，界面布局应自动调整。即将浏览型内容上移，在上半屏显示；将操作类控件元素下沉，在下半屏显示。提供更舒适和高效的使用体验。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p1119849175217"><strong>视频通话</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p430mcpsimp">悬停时，上半屏显示通话界面，下半屏显示通话相关的操作按钮。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p072342524115"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163731.10862842494926056564991190740698:50001231000000:2800:55695F425B6BC65653381009CD25E6E551D93BC623FA2CFB4C93188F984FCE3D.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p39581525105518"></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p2037615282551"><strong>视频</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p354mcpsimp">悬停时，上半屏显示视频画面，下半屏显示视频相关的操作按钮或周边信息。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p31431948184110"><span><img originheight="2160" originwidth="4320" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251120163731.76743956651805709142132678901907:50001231000000:2800:ADCE3BE81F6D4AFBBBDDE3EBB71DA540702C43343FAD70C58375C28FFFF30FEE.png" title="点击放大" width="920" height="460"></span></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p165334565610"></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p149615555619"><strong>短视频</strong></p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p229mcpsimp">短视频悬停时，头像、评论、视频画面等显示的内容在上半屏展示，输入框等操作在下半屏显示。短视频类应用进行需要手势操作快速切换视频内容。建议下半屏支持横向滑动切换视频。</p>     <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002352875141__p926118417423">      </p><div class="video-box" style="width: 920px; height: 458.16px;"><div
